116 今、天王星のwiki見てきたら軌道傾斜角(i) が0.774°だった (ﾜｯﾁｮｲ d3c5-7e6N) 2023/06/16(金) 04:03:45.33
 &gt;&gt;114 <br> ■現状デフォルトで下記チェック入っているから(((…)))と[[[…]]]は今でも使える前提 <br> Setting &gt; Stable Diffusion &gt; Emphasis: use (text) to make model pay more attention to text and [text] to make it pay less attention <br> https://i.imgur.com/ViHyUBo.png <br>  <br> ■Setting &gt; Compatibility &gt; Use old emphasis implementation. Can be useful to reproduce old seeds. <br> を使うのは <br> Promptの一部を無視してしまうエラーがあった2022年9月29日までの旧バージョンAUTOMATIC1111で作った画像を再現するときに使うやつや <br> 下記後半部参照 <br> https://github.com/AUTOMATIC1111/stable-diffusion-webui/wiki/Features#attentionemphasis <br> On 2022-09-29, a new implementation was added that supports escape characters and numerical weights. A downside of the new implementation is that the old one was not perfect and sometimes ate characters: &quot;a (((farm))), daytime&quot;, for example, would become &quot;a farm daytime&quot; without the comma. This behavior is not shared by the new implementation which preserves all text correctly, and this means that your saved seeds may produce different pictures. For now, there is an option in settings to use the old implementation.
